Kuhn</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wayback_Machine" title="Wayback Machine">互联网档案馆</a>的<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20150417031348/http://www.britannica.com/EBchecked/topic/324460/Thomas-S-Kuhn" rel="nofollow">存檔</a>，存档日期2015-04-17.. </li>
<li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"<i>Pseudoscientific – pretending to be scientific, falsely represented as being scientific</i>", from the <i>Oxford American Dictionary</i>, published by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oxford_English_Dictionary" title="Oxford English Dictionary">Oxford English Dictionary</a>; Hansson, Sven Ove (1996)."Defining Pseudoscience", Philosophia Naturalis, 33: 169–176, as cited in <a class="external text" href="http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/pseudo-science/#NonSciPosSci" rel="nofollow">"Science and Pseudo-science"</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20150905091332/http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/pseudo-science/" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>） (2008) in Stanford Encyclopedia of Philosophy. The Stanford article states: "Many writers on pseudoscience have emphasized that pseudoscience is non-science posing as science. The foremost modern classic on the subject (Gardner 1957) bears the title <span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fads and Fallacies in the Name of Science" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="以科學為名義的潮流與謬論"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%A5%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8%E7%82%BA%E5%90%8D%E7%BE%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%BD%AE%E6%B5%81%E8%88%87%E8%AC%AC%E8%AB%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="以科學為名義的潮流與謬論（页面不存在）">Fads and Fallacies in the Name of Science</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fads_and_Fallacies_in_the_Name_of_Science" title="en:Fads and Fallacies in the Name of Science"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fads and Fallacies in the Name of Science</span></a></span>）</span></span>. According to Brian Baigrie (1988, 438), "[w]hat is objectionable about these beliefs is that they masquerade as genuinely scientific ones." These and many other authors assume that to be pseudoscientific, an activity or a teaching has to satisfy the following two criteria (Hansson 1996): (1) it is not scientific, and (2) its major proponents try to create the impression that it is scientific".

<ul><li>For example, Hewitt et al. <i>Conceptual Physical Science</i> Addison Wesley; 3 edition (July 18, 2003) <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9780321051738">ISBN 978-0-321-05173-8</a>, Bennett et al. <i>The Cosmic Perspective</i> 3e Addison Wesley; 3 edition (July 25, 2003) <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9780805387384">ISBN 978-0-8053-8738-4</a>; <i>See also</i>, e.g., Gauch HG Jr. <i>Scientific Method in Practice</i> (2003).</li>
<li>A 2006 <a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%9F%BA%E9%87%91%E4%BC%9A" title="国家科学基金会">National Science Foundation</a> report on Science and engineering indicators quoted <span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Michael Shermer" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="麥克·雪爾默"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BA%A5%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E9%9B%AA%E7%88%BE%E9%BB%98&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="麥克·雪爾默（页面不存在）">Michael Shermer</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Shermer" title="en:Michael Shermer"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Michael Shermer</span></a></span>）</span></span>'s (1997) definition of pseudoscience: '"claims presented so that they appear [to be] scientific even though they lack supporting evidence and plausibility"(p. 33). In contrast, science is "a set of methods designed to describe and interpret observed and inferred phenomena, past or present, and aimed at building a testable body of knowledge open to rejection or confirmation"(p. 17)'.<cite class="citation book">Shermer M. Why People Believe Weird Things: Pseudoscience, Superstition, and Other Confusions of Our Time. New York: W. H. Freeman and Company. 1997. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0-7167-3090-1" title="Special:网络书源/0-7167-3090-1"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 0-7167-3090-1</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6&amp;rft.au=Shermer+M.&amp;rft.btitle=Why+People+Believe+Weird+Things%3A+Pseudoscience%2C+Superstition%2C+and+Other+Confusions+of+Our+Time&amp;rft.date=1997&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=0-7167-3090-1&amp;rft.place=New+York&amp;rft.pub=W.+H.+Freeman+and+Company&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span> as cited by <cite class="citation book"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Science_Foundation" title="National Science Foundation">National Science Foundation</a>; Division of Science Resources Statistics. Science and Technology: Public Attitudes and Understanding. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nsf.gov/statistics/seind06/c7/c7s2.htm" rel="nofollow">Science and engineering indicators 2006</a>. 2006 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2015-10-01</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://www.webcitation.org/617VmAeHP?url=http://www.nsf.gov/statistics/seind06/c7/c7s2.htm" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2011-08-22）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6&amp;rft.atitle=Science+and+Technology%3A+Public+Attitudes+and+Understanding&amp;rft.au=Division+of+Science+Resources+Statistics&amp;rft.au=National+Science+Foundation&amp;rft.btitle=Science+and+engineering+indicators+2006&amp;rft.date=2006&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.nsf.gov%2Fstatistics%2Fseind06%2Fc7%2Fc7s2.htm&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>
<li>"A pretended or spurious science; a collection of related beliefs about the world mistakenly regarded as being based on scientific method or as having the status that scientific truths now have," from the <i><a href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E6%B4%A5%E8%8B%B1%E8%AA%9E%E8%A9%9E%E5%85%B8" title="牛津英語詞典">Oxford English Dictionary</a></i>, second edition 1989.</li></ul>
</span></li>

<ul><li><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E6%B3%A2%E6%99%AE%E5%B0%94" title="卡尔·波普尔">Popper, Karl</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/?id=fZnrUfJWQ-YC&amp;printsec=frontcover&amp;dq=conjectures+and+refutations" rel="nofollow">Conjectures and Refutations</a>. <li id="cite_note-First_Scientist,_Clegg-27"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-First_Scientist,_Clegg_27-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">results, search. <a class="external text" href="https://www.amazon.com/First-Scientist-Life-Roger-Bacon/dp/0786713585/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1372950566&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=Roger+Bacon" rel="nofollow">The First Scientist: A Life of Roger Bacon</a> Reprint edition. Da Capo Press. 2004-06-20 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2017-04-26</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9780786713585" title="Special:网络书源/9780786713585"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9780786713585</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210516174957/https://www.amazon.com/First-Scientist-Life-Roger-Bacon/dp/0786713585/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1372950566&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=Roger+Bacon" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2021-05-16） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到英语网页">（英语）</span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6&amp;rft.aufirst=search&amp;rft.aulast=results&amp;rft.btitle=The+First+Scientist%3A+A+Life+of+Roger+Bacon&amp;rft.date=2004-06-20&amp;rft.edition=Reprint+edition&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9780786713585&amp;rft.pub=Da+Capo+Press&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.amazon.com%2FFirst-Scientist-Life-Roger-Bacon%2Fdp%2F0786713585%2Fref%3Dsr_1_1%3Fs%3Dbooks%26ie%3DUTF8%26qid%3D1372950566%26sr%3D1-1%26keywords%3DRoger%2BBacon&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span><span class="citation-comment" style="display:none; color:#33aa33"> 引文格式1维护：冗余文本 (<a href="/wiki/Category:%E5%BC%95%E6%96%87%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F1%E7%BB%B4%E6%8A%A4%EF%BC%9A%E5%86%97%E4%BD%99%E6%96%87%E6%9C%AC" title="Category:引文格式1维护：冗余文本">link</a>)</span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-28"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-28">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%97%E5%85%B0%E8%A5%BF%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E5%9F%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="弗兰西斯·培根">Bacon, Francis</a> <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%B7%A5%E5%85%B7" title="新工具">Novum Organum</a> (The New Organon)</i>, 1620. Bacon's work described many of the accepted principles, underscoring the importance of empirical results, data gathering and experiment.  <i>Encyclopædia Britannica</i> (1911), "<a class="extiw" href="https://zh.wikisource.org/wiki/1911_Encyclop%C3%A6dia_Britannica/Bacon,_Francis" title="s:1911 Encyclopædia Britannica/Bacon, Francis">Bacon, Francis</a>" states: [In Novum Organum, we ] "proceed to apply what is perhaps the most valuable part of the Baconian method, the process of exclusion or rejection. This elimination of the non-essential, ... , is the most important of Bacon's contributions to the logic of induction, and that in which, as he repeatedly says, his method differs from all previous philosophies."</span>
</li>

<li id="cite_note-Friedman-pxiv-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Friedman-pxiv_31-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Michael Friedman, <i>Reconsidering Logical Positivism</i> (New York: Cambridge University Press, 1999), <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=e9TjZc9wNUAC&amp;pg=PR14" rel="nofollow">p xiv</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20160628112455/https://books.google.com/books?id=e9TjZc9wNUAC&amp;pg=PR14" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-autogenerated1-32"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-autogenerated1_32-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">See <a class="external text" href="http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/vienna-circle" rel="nofollow">"Vienna Circle"</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20150810041731/http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/vienna-circle" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>） in <i>Stanford Encyclopedia of Philosophy</i>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Smith1986-33"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Smith1986_33-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Smith, L.D. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=IZ6aAAAAIAAJ&amp;pg=PA314" rel="nofollow">Behaviorism and Logical Positivism: A Reassessment of the Alliance</a>. Stanford University Press. 1986: 314 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2017-04-26</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-8047-1301-6" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-8047-1301-6"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-0-8047-1301-6</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://lccn.loc.gov/85030366" rel="nofollow"><span title="美国国会图书馆控制码">LCCN 85030366</span></a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160501142803/https://books.google.com/books?id=IZ6aAAAAIAAJ&amp;pg=PA314" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2016-05-01）. <q>The secondary and historical literature on logical positivism affords substantial grounds for concluding that logical positivism failed to solve many of the central problems it generated for itself. Prominent among the unsolved problems was the failure to find an acceptable statement of the verifiability (later confirmability) criterion of meaningfulness. Until a competing tradition emerged (about the late 1950's), the problems of logical positivism continued to be attacked from within that tradition. But as the new tradition in the philosophy of science began to demonstrate its effectiveness—by dissolving and rephrasing old problems as well as by generating new ones—philosophers began to shift allegiances to the new tradition, even though that tradition has yet to receive a canonical formulation.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6&amp;rft.aufirst=L.D.&amp;rft.aulast=Smith&amp;rft.btitle=Behaviorism+and+Logical+Positivism%3A+A+Reassessment+of+the+Alliance&amp;rft.date=1986&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-8047-1301-6&amp;rft.pages=314&amp;rft.pub=Stanford+University+Press&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DIZ6aAAAAIAAJ%26pg%3DPA314&amp;rft_id=info%3Alccn%2F85030366&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Bunge1996-34"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Bunge1996_34-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Bunge, M.A. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=8YAV43gVMsIC&amp;pg=PA317" rel="nofollow">Finding Philosophy in Social Science</a>. Yale University Press. 1996: 317 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2017-04-26</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-300-06606-7" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-300-06606-7"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-0-300-06606-7</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://lccn.loc.gov/lc96004399" rel="nofollow"><span title="美国国会图书馆控制码">LCCN lc96004399</span></a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160604053509/https://books.google.com/books?id=8YAV43gVMsIC&amp;pg=PA317" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2016-06-04）. <q>To conclude, logical positivism was progressive compared with the classical positivism of <a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E5%8A%B3%E7%8B%84%E4%B9%8C%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%89%98%E5%8B%92%E5%AF%86" title="克劳狄乌斯·托勒密">Ptolemy</a>, <a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E5%8D%AB%C2%B7%E4%BC%91%E8%B0%9F" title="大卫·休谟">Hume</a>, d'Alembert, Compte, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E5%8F%B2%E9%83%BD%E8%8F%AF%C2%B7%E5%BD%8C%E7%88%BE" title="約翰·史都華·彌爾">John Stuart Mill</a>, and <a href="/wiki/%E6%81%A9%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%C2%B7%E9%A9%AC%E8%B5%AB" title="恩斯特·马赫">Ernst Mach</a>. It was even more so by comparison with its contemporary rivals—neo-Thomisism, <a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%BA%B7%E5%BE%B7%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89" title="新康德主义">neo-Kantianism</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%89%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89" title="数学直觉主义">intuitionism</a>, dialectical materialism, phenomenology, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E4%B8%BB%E7%BE%A9" title="存在主義">existentialism</a>. However, neo-positivism failed dismally to give a faithful account of science, whether natural or social. It failed because it remained anchored to sense-data and to a phenomenalist metaphysics, overrated the power of induction and underrated that of hypothesis, and denounced realism and materialism as metaphysical nonsense. Although it has never been practiced consistently in the advanced natural sciences and has been criticized by many philosophers, notably Popper (1959 [1935], 1963), logical positivism remains the tacit philosophy of many scientists. Regrettably, the anti-positivism fashionable in the metatheory of social science is often nothing but an excuse for sloppiness and wild speculation.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6&amp;rft.aufirst=M.A.&amp;rft.aulast=Bunge&amp;rft.btitle=Finding+Philosophy+in+Social+Science&amp;rft.date=1996&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-300-06606-7&amp;rft.pages=317&amp;rft.pub=Yale+University+Press&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D8YAV43gVMsIC%26pg%3DPA317&amp;rft_id=info%3Alccn%2Flc96004399&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-35"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-35">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20140107230818/http://www.drury.edu/ess/philsci/popper.html" rel="nofollow">Popper, Falsifiability, and the Failure of Positivism</a>. 2000-08-07 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2014-01-07</span>]</span>. （<a class="external text" href="http://www.drury.edu/ess/philsci/popper.html" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2014-01-07）. <q>The upshot is that the positivists seem caught between insisting on the V.C. [Verifiability Criterion]—but for no defensible reason—or admitting that the V.C. requires a background language, etc., which opens the door to relativism, etc. In light of this dilemma, many folk—especially following Popper's "last-ditch" effort to "save" empiricism/positivism/realism with the falsifiability criterion—have agreed that positivism is a dead-end.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6&amp;rft.btitle=Popper%2C+Falsifiability%2C+and+the+Failure+of+Positivism&amp;rft.date=2000-08-07&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.drury.edu%2Fess%2Fphilsci%2Fpopper.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Friedman-pxii-36"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Friedman-pxii_36-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Friedman, <i>Reconsidering Logical Positivism</i> (Cambridge U P, 1999), <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=e9TjZc9wNUAC&amp;pg=PR12" rel="nofollow">p xii</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20160628220109/https://books.google.com/books?id=e9TjZc9wNUAC&amp;pg=PR12" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）.</span>

<li id="cite_note-Popper_2005ch3-4-42"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Popper_2005ch3-4_42-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Popper, Karl. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books/about/The_Logic_of_Scientific_Discovery.html" rel="nofollow">The Logic of Scientific Discovery</a> Taylor &amp; Francis e-Library.
